href="https://newsofx2.com/dvam-domestic-violence-awareness-month-hell/" rel="bookmark">DVAM (Domestic Violence Awareness Month): Hell</a></h2><div class="entry-meta">
<span class="posted-on"><time class="updated" datetime="2025-05-19T18:07:16+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">May 19, 2025</time><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-03-14T07:02:08+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">March 14, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://newsofx2.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">
<a href="https://newsofx2.com/dvam-domestic-violence-awareness-month-hell/">
<img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODdhAQABAPAAAMPDwwAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs=" width="820" height="480" data-src="https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="DVAM (Domestic Violence Awareness Month): Hell" itemprop="image" decoding="async" data-srcset="https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell.jpg 820w, https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell-300x176.jpg 300w, https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell-768x450.jpg 768w" data-sizes="(max-width: 820px) 100vw, 820px" /><noscript><img width="820" height="480" src="https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="DVAM (Domestic Violence Awareness Month): Hell" itemprop="image" decoding="async" srcset="https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell.jpg 820w, https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell-300x176.jpg 300w, https://newsofx2.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/DVAM-Domestic-Violence-Awareness-Month-Hell-768x450.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 820px) 100vw, 820px" /></noscript>
</a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>Every October is Domestic Violence Awareness Month (DVAM) in the United States. Why has DV gotten even worse since implementing this awareness program two decades ago? Martin Luther King said it best, &#8220;You can&#8217;t fight lies with worse lies or fight hate with worse hate.&#8221; DVAM is pure hate and lies and thus makes the &#8230; <a title="DVAM (Domestic Violence Awareness Month): Hell" class="read-more" href="https://newsofx2.com/dvam-domestic-violence-awareness-month-hell/" aria-label="Read more about DVAM (Domestic Violence Awareness Month): Hell">Read more</a></p></div><footer class="entry-meta" aria-label="Entry meta">
